    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText4198369975066576326" style="display:none">THE STUNNING CONCLUSION TO THE THIS MAN TRILOGY!<br /><br />The Manor, the very place where their passionate love affair began, fills with guests on what should be the happiest day of Ava and Jesse's lives. She has accepted that she'll never tame the fierceness in Jesse-and she doesn't want to. Their love is profound, their connection powerful, but just when she thinks that she's finally gotten beneath his guarded exterior, more questions arise, leading Ava to believe that Jesse Ward may not be the man she thinks he is. He knows too well how to take her to a place beyond ecstasy . . . but will he also drive her to the brink of despair? It's time for this man to confess.</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">It's a hard question to answer because technically he had left her. Do you remember in This Man when he got fed up and just left her for 4 days withou<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">It's a hard question to answer because technically he had left her. Do you remember in This Man when he got fed up and just left her for 4 days without any word? It was sometime during those 4 days that he slept with Coral. I'm not sure if they were technically in a relationship at the time though, because even Ava wasn't sure what their status was at the time.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer508855747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14379116882859484451"><a href='https://www.amazon.co.uk/dp/B00DQUXAGM' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Live NOW at Amazon UK</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405517i/790035._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo tmconfessed_zps20dde3de.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jodi Ellen Malpas first appeared on our horizons in October 2012 with a fairly quiet release for This Man which began, rapidly, to snowball as readers, reviewers and bloggers all started to rave about this wonderful, bossy, demanding and a little bit crazy new hero – Jesse Ward, Lord of the Sex Manor. By the time January came around anticipation for the release of the second book in the trilogy, Beneath This Man, had reached fever pitch and it’s no different this time as we’</span>
  <span id="freeText14379116882859484451" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.amazon.co.uk/dp/B00DQUXAGM" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Live NOW at Amazon UK</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405517i/790035._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo tmconfessed_zps20dde3de.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jodi Ellen Malpas first appeared on our horizons in October 2012 with a fairly quiet release for This Man which began, rapidly, to snowball as readers, reviewers and bloggers all started to rave about this wonderful, bossy, demanding and a little bit crazy new hero – Jesse Ward, Lord of the Sex Manor. By the time January came around anticipation for the release of the second book in the trilogy, Beneath This Man, had reached fever pitch and it’s no different this time as we’ve waited with bated breath for the thrilling conclusion to this amazing trilogy and let me take a moment here to lay some of your anxieties to rest. This Man Confessed is just about everything you could have ever possibly hoped it would be and yet more.<br><br>This was really very special. I was so looking forward to losing myself once again in Jesse and Ava’s sexy world and it absolutely didn’t disappoint. For me, this erotic trilogy stands above ALL others. I love Jesse and Ava SO much, I feel so incredibly connected to them and I am now finding it hard to let go. I’ve got to know them so well, become so invested in their story that they have become quite simply unforgettable. They’ll be an incredibly hard act to follow and this book most probably will leave you with the book hangover to end all book hangovers. I know it did for me!<br><br> <br><br>I read slowly, trying to savour every word, sadly watching the progress on my Kindle edge ever closer to 100% knowing that I was going to be leaving Jesse &amp; Ava behind, not wanting to part with them. The sun even graced me with its presence as I read this one, something that doesn’t happen very often in England, and I now have the fondest memories of reading this one sprawled on a sun lounger, completely lost in their world as reality just fell away and all that existed for me were the words on the page. Not many books are able to do this to me – this one really is that special.<br><br>Jesse is back in all his fresh water minty loveliness, Lord of the Sex Manor, an impossible, bossy, demanding, uber-possessive, neurotic yet so very, very sexy ex-playboy. He’s still overbearing, unreasonable, challenging but, heck, how much do I love him?<br><br><br>Ava’s still swearing like a sailor and prompting Jesse to yell at her to watch her mouth. The sense fucks, reminder fucks, sleepy sex – they’re all back to be joined by the compromise fuck and sleepy twilight sex. We have incredibly ambient kinky sex at The Manor, a super sexy game of strip poker and, as usual, Jesse is confidently dominant and trying hard to stay in charge.<br><br><br>This is an angst ridden journey with lots of shocks and gasp out loud moments and plenty of despair for the two of them which all makes their Happy Ever After all the sweeter. Jesse has a troubled history full of pain, guilt and sorrow that he will finally confess to and Ava is helping to heal all that hurt and suffering. She’s his little piece of heaven and she’ll never allow him to fall back into that harsh, hollow past but you can be sure that if there’s an easy way to do things, Jesse &amp; Ava won’t do it this way as we embark on yet another rollercoaster of a journey with them. They’re both incredibly argumentative and both want their own way and they’re always quick to anger and shout at each other and watch out for a thrilling, pulsating conclusion so enthralling that I could hardly breathe as I read it – thankfully all followed by a wonderful epilogue.<br><br>This is, quite simply, just a beautiful love story. It all felt so incredibly real to me – nobody is perfect, everybody has flaws, they face difficulties together, they scream and yell at each other, fight like cat and dog, overcome those difficulties together and, most importantly, they love one another wholeheartedly and, however painful that seems to be, that is the overriding factor here – the central theme to the whole wonderful story that is the This Man trilogy.<br><br>Jesse is incredibly intense – oh to be on the receiving end of all that intensity that is Jesse Ward. His love for Ava has completely overwhelmed him and he is terrified that he could lose her and this is what's causing all this protectiveness and his possessiveness that is driving Ava crazy! This may well be the most beautiful love story ever written.<br><br>I very much enjoyed the writing style and I feel like I’ve been in safe hands – I felt that this story was meticulously mapped out and that Jodi knew from the very first page of This Man, exactly where this story was going, where every character fitted in and how it was all going to end. The story and characters strayed true throughout and this, for me, is the hallmark of a talented writer. Even though I am sad to leave behind Jesse &amp; Ava, I am looking forward to whatever Jodi does next. I’ll definitely be reading it.<br> <br><br>So, in conclusion, this is quite possibly the best erotic romance trilogy EVER written, the most intense hero I think you will ever read and this book is up there contending for my book of the year for 2013. This is special – you are all going to love it.<br><br>5 sexy as fuck stars!<br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

  <span id="freeText3811737528994197474" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS ... END OF.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422616i/841141._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422616i/841142._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I finally got my hands on 'This man confessed' and i'm still riding on central Jesse cloud nine. I have never been more excited about a release of a book, the story of Jesse and Ava and there unrelenting relationship wraps up in this epic finale and I worshipped every page.<br><br>Jodi ellen Malpas goes on my list of favourite authors she has two hugely redeeming qualities, number one: she is gorgeously British and proud of it, delivering (and not apologising for) her wonderful British-isms and number two: she delivered to the world Jesse Ward, a character never to be forgotten and never to be created again, so with all that gushing being said here are my over zealous book thoughts, welcome to 'This man confessed' as seen through my eyes ...<br><br><b>What's it all about ...</b><br>Well if you have got to this point and still haven't realised 'This man confessed' is the last book in a trilogy where we are thrown into the world of Jesse Ward and Ava O'Shea. At his point we have been through a myriad of ups and downs to form one hugely epic love story. 'This man confessed' takes right off from its predecessor 'Beneath this man', Jesse and Ava are now taking steps to further their relationship and commitment to each other, the story continues to uncover secrets, future stumbling blocks and more sexual encounters than you could shake a stick at. <br><br><b>What I loved?</b><br>To start with I was impressed with the consistency of story, and character development. The author stays true to the original premise and I found her writing continually witty and engaging. I can't deny that the biggest pull for me in this trilogy is Mr Jesse Ward, hands off readers he's MINE, I can't gush or talk favourably enough about this fictional hero, he's as sexy as he is infuriating and I'm more than a little sad to say goodbye. I also loved the drama and suspense of the series, secrets were popping out about the characters right until the end, this author knows how to keep her readers entertained. This book hands, feet and any other body parts that you want to put down has the sweetest, most gorgeous epilogue I've ever read, I left this story with a huge smile and a hankering for more of this authors writing.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422616i/841143._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>The final book in a trilogy is always tinged with a little sadness for me, when you invest in characters and love what an author does to make a story come alive, it is inevitable that the reader wants to savour the last moments. I couldn't have enjoyed this conclusion more, if you haven't started this series ... What are you waiting for jump aboard readers you won't won't to get off central Jesse cloud nine.<br><br>With all that laid out on the table, you know I love this series and Mr Jesse Ward our impossible, overbearing, demanding, unreasonable but equally gorgeous, commanding and protective lord of the manor ... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422616i/841144._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Re read anyone?</b><br><br>*A HUGE kiss and THANK YOU to my Goodreads girls, Christy and the Pink Ladies for the buddy read, we share a love for Jesse Ward together and I LOVED it ... Watch your fcuking mouths ladies.*</span>

  <span id="freeText13182168381162448413" style="display:none">I just. Why. Why did I read this. Why. Why did I keep going. Why don't any of my friends like me enough to take me aside and tell me to stop hating myself and take some time to love me enough to stop punishing myself with terrible books that I know are only going to cause me agony? WHY DON'T YOU LIKE ME, FRIENDS? YOU COULD SEE ME OVER HERE WITH THE BOOK. WHY, FRIENDS? WHY? I THOUGHT WE WERE FRIENDS, FRIENDS.<br><br>Just don't read any farther than this if you don't want to know anything about these books, okay? <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[- Jesse and Ava are still both the worst people on the entire planet. She deliberately does things to make him angry in fits of pique. They stay together even despite continually mounting evidence that they bring out the ABSOLUTE WORST in each other. How many people have to tell Ava, "Oh, yeah, Jesse's the most laid back guy in the world," and she's like, "Uh, I don't know that guy," until she realizes, "MAYBE I MAKE MY HUSBAND INTO A MONSTER" and also for her to realize that when she deliberately, oh, I don't know, RUBS HER VAGINA ALL UP ON ANOTHER DUDE TO MAKE HIM MAD, she also isn't being a lovely person when she's with him?<br><br>- And yet, it's not that I think that all characters have to be likable people, because they don't. Characters being bad people is fine, because it's the author's choice to make. It's just that the author chose to make these two people COMPLETE SHITHEADS, and then illustrate them being COMPLETE SHITHEADS in the same pattern SIXTY FOUR TIMES with absolutely no variation or redemption.<br><br>- AND THEN. FINALLY SOME RELIEF FROM THE SPACKLED ON PILL FORESHADOWING. But it's fine-ish, right, because these days, it's all a competition about who can write the most Alpha-y-ist Alpha, and it's ROMANTIC, really, that he wanted to steal her pills to keep her around forever, fine, whatever, and even though Ava has known for HOW LONG by the point he finally tells her, NOW SHE decides to get mad, like with the whole Sarah thing, where she knows stuff but for some reason can't just USE HER ADULT WORDS, and leaves, and finds out she's pregnant, and tells Jesse she's not (NOT OKAY) and schedules an abortion without telling her husband (REALLY NOT OKAY) and then goes out drinking... <br><br>and this is where the author crosses the line for me into making Ava into just a... what? What is Ava? I mean, as a character? She's still a NOTHING! As far as character traits, I mean. Why do two dudes want her? She's just shitty, all around. Just awful and shitty and terrible. She doesn't seem smart, or funny, or interesting, or any good at all. She's just a convenient mouthpiece for whatever twists and turns the author wants done at any given moment in the plot. She's worse than nothing. She's just a doll or a prop for the author. If there's any development at all in this book, it's gone into Jesse, and Ava's just a floppy cock holster for Jesse's enormous wang that has the magical capabilities to make nothing Ava orgasm on command. Or at least, I assume it still does, since I started skimming the ridiculous, convoluted, and impossible to picture/grasp/comprehend sex scenes way back in book one, because ha. No.<br><br>- Matt. Yeah, that gets sealed up and tossed aside way back in the beginning. Guess we were done with him.<br><br>- The thing with Coral. What a poorly written scene. I had to keep reading it over and over and still didn't actually grasp who was holding what paper and who was showing what to who. I mean, I get that super brilliant Ava actually totally figured out what was going on with her super duper mom instincts and SOLVED THE CASE right there with her Special Eyes, but actually grocking what was happening physically in the scene? No. Could not.<br><br>- Mikael. Oh, shut the fuck up. I can't even make a solid case in this book for ONE person falling for rag doll nothing blob Ava on sight, let alone two. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I can't stand to read one more book NOT ONE MORE BOOK where everything the author has is poured into developing the dude and then you look over at the lady he's supposedly head over heels for and...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/226645.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>COME ON. She's not just there to advance your plot, she's a CHARACTER, TOO. She's got to be SOMETHING WORTHWHILE for it to be believable that this amazing guy that 98% of the book's resources are put toward detailing, or he's only 12% amazing, 88% idiot. HE CAN'T BE THAT AWESOME IF HE'S FOLLOWING HIS PENIS INTO A BIG CAVERN VAGINA OF COTTON CANDY AND MUPPET ARMS.<br><br>PARDON MY TANTRUM, I JUST FOUND OUT NONE OF MY FRIENDS LIKE ME.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13182168381162448413" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_657245647" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/657245647" />
    <a title="Miss H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h"><img alt="Miss H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475977422p2/15490946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/657245647?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss H" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h">Miss H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=smutty-reads">smutty-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=douch-canoe-hero">douch-canoe-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=unlikeable-characters">unlikeable-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=damaged-heroes-heroines">damaged-heroes-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=hero-not-celibate-during-separation">hero-not-celibate-during-separation</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=kill-it-with-fire">kill-it-with-fire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=please-fire-your-editor">please-fire-your-editor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=hated-this-book">hated-this-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer657245647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5742687300739193681">This review is likely to contain spoilers, by which I mean they’re everywhere. <br/><br/>If I could give this book zero stars, I would.<br/><br/>I don’t know what I was thinking when I decided it’d be a good idea to read this. I mean, after all, I wasn’t exactly a fan of the first two books. Can I plead temporary insanity? I’m going to chalk it up to it being one of those cases where it was so bad I couldn’t stop reading—and that goes for the trilogy as a whole. Apparently, it would seem, I’m an even bigger glutton</span>
  <span id="freeText5742687300739193681" style="display:none">This review is likely to contain spoilers, by which I mean they’re everywhere. <br><br>If I could give this book zero stars, I would.<br><br>I don’t know what I was thinking when I decided it’d be a good idea to read this. I mean, after all, I wasn’t exactly a fan of the first two books. Can I plead temporary insanity? I’m going to chalk it up to it being one of those cases where it was so bad I couldn’t stop reading—and that goes for the trilogy as a whole. Apparently, it would seem, I’m an even bigger glutton for punishment.<br><br>Anyway, I’m just going to jump right in.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427686ra/855103.gif" width="245" height="245" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This drivel is not romance. Nothing about this book, or trilogy rather, is romantic by any stretch of the imagination.<br><br><i>This Man Confessed</i> opens up on the day of Ava’s wedding—two whole weeks after the end of <i>Beneath This Man</i>. As usual, Jesse has gotten his way. Shocking, I know. They’re getting married at the Manor. Ava has had no involvement in any of the wedding planning, no input whatsoever. No shower or bachelorette party for this bride-to-be. She’s rather blasé about the whole affair. I guess that’s to be expected since, you know, she’s too busy worrying about her unsuspecting family stumbling upon something they’re not supposed to see like, say, an orgy. They’re under the impression that the wedding is taking place at Jesse’s country retreat. Ava’s poor mom is so clueless and proud of the venue, praising it to the high heavens, that she’s taken to giving tours to wedding guests.<br><br>By this point, I was already bored. It was a lesson in patience just to get through the wedding day. It was overly long and boring, if I’m being honest. It was multiple chapters of nothing but filler: preparations, Jesse acting his usual psychotic self, drama on top of drama, and a million other useless things, only for the actual wedding to be glossed over—but not before we get to watch Jesse march down the aisle to snatch Ava from her father’s arms and handcuff himself to her. Up until that point, I thought, just for a moment, that Ava would finally see the light, smarten up, and leave his crazy-ass at the altar. Then I thought, “Who am I kidding?” Next thing you know, the scene skips to the reception, where more crazy antics ensue.<br><br>Speaking of crazy antics, why are Ava and Kate friends again? Kate is one of the worst friends imaginable. She can’t even manage to be a decent maid of honor. She was drunk long before the wedding even began. At one point, during the reception, Ava escapes to the bathroom, only to discover that Kate is busy having sex in one of the stalls and the guy most certainly isn’t Sam, her current boyfriend.<br><br>I was pretty much disgusted with Ava’s behavior from start to finish. After Jesse confesses to stealing her birth control pills, which she already knew, she finally decides to get mad. She rants and raves about how she doesn’t want a baby and “how dare he do this to her?” I like how she puts the blame all on him, as if she wasn’t a willing participant each and every time they had unprotected sex. Let’s not pretend it was a one-time incident either. It happened on numerous occasions, multiple times a day. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/534355.gif" width="400" height="228" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As is her habit, she does the mature thing by running away from her problems because, yes, that clearly solves everything. Before she leaves her new husband, she slaps him across the face. By the way, they haven’t even been married an entire week by this point. She eventually gets it together enough to have her pregnancy confirmed, for all the good it does. Without an ounce of regret or remorse, she lies to Jesse about the results. Later, back at Kate’s place, where she’s been staying, she treats herself to a big glass of wine, her first of many throughout the book. Her life is horrible, don’t you know? Being married to a billionaire is hard work. Never mind the fact that she will never want for anything, has the job of her dreams and, oh yeah, she’s knocked up. She deserves a drink, dammit. To hell with being pregnant. Kate being the smart, awesome friend that she is, decides to help get Ava out of her funk by taking her to a bar, where Ava gets completely wasted. I’m talking stumbling, falling-down drunk.<br><br>I can understand her initial shock about the pregnancy, but at the same time, given her strong reaction to the news, throwing a pity party for herself by indulging in alcohol as a way of revenge does little in the way of her likeability. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427686ra/855104.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This is Ava we’re talking about, however. We all know she won’t stay mad for long and will run back to Jesse before it’s all said and done, where they'll find something else to fight about. Rise and repeat.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427686ra/855105.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Both before and after they reconcile, several chapters are dedicated to Ava’s incessant whining about how her pregnancy has ruined her life. The most important of which is the fact that she can no longer perform oral sex without getting sick. She turns it into such a big deal, you’d think the world was coming to an end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427686ra/855106.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think most of my dislike boils down to the fact that Ava is a terrible heroine. She possesses more bad traits than good. It seems all she’s capable of is drinking, arguing with Jesse, being a pushover, and getting easily deceived.<br><br><i>This Man Confessed</i> is aptly named. Jesse confesses to so many things, many of which seem to come straight out of left field, that it was hard to keep track of them all. Each confession is somehow more outrageous and ridiculous than the one before it. It seemed like the author was trying too hard to redeem him, to excuse away his overabundance of crazy, to somehow make his behavior okay. I’m sorry, but that’s a little hard to do when I read a scene like this:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“‘Zero, baby.’ I’m snatched from my chair before my brain filters the final call of the countdown, and I’m on the floor, wrists pinned above my head and Jesse straddling my waist. My eyes are wide and the restaurant is silent. You could hear a pin drop. I’m staring up at Jesse, who is unashamed and most unconcerned by our surroundings. He’s got me sprawled on the floor in a restaurant. What the fucking hell is he playing at? I dare not even look away from him. I can feel a million sets of shocked eyes drilling into the spectacle Jesse has created. I’m mortified. <br><br>‘Jesse, let me up.’ I wouldn’t put much past him, but this? This is way past unashamed. Fucking hell, what if someone tries to pull him off me? <br><br>‘I did warn you, baby.’ His face is awash with amusement, while I’m simply horrified. ‘Wherever, whenever.’”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440037255ra/15921364.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, that’s totally normal. There’s nothing wrong with a grown man physically restraining his pregnant wife by sitting on her (more or less) in the middle of a crowded restaurant until she relents to whatever it is he’s demanding of her. Is this simpleton for real? Her only concern is to question what may or may not happen should someone come to her aid. These two not only deserve each other, but they both belong in the loony bin.<br><br>I never thought I’d say this, but the excessive amount of sex was not to my liking. Several pages were dedicated to each scene, and trust me, there were plenty. It was as if the book was stuck in a repetitive loop. It became so tedious that I started skimming/skipping them altogether. Don’t even get me started on the drama. There was so much, most of it manufactured, that I was a little dazed by the time I finished reading. It was like a soap opera on steroids.<br><br>As with the other two books, the editing could use some work, but I guess that’s par for the course.<br><br>The epilogue, told from Jesse’s point of view, was awkward. I don’t know many five-year-olds who talk as if they’re fully-grown. The little boy is already a mini Jesse: “Mummy! Watch your mouth!” Needless to say, there were plenty of cringe-worthy moments to be had while reading their happily ever after.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5742687300739193681" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_509171407" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509171407" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/509171407?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509171407" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7989977693818195582"><b>5 Lord of the Manor Loving Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/7563fe7a-5665-4266-b8aa-7fcc7d40f0a1_zpsb654e5fb.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790296.jpg' alt=' photo 7563fe7a-5665-4266-b8aa-7fcc7d40f0a1_zpsb654e5fb.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So it’s Monday night at midnight... what am I doing? Thats right, I am awake clicking the refresh screen on amazon to see if ‘This Man Confessed’ is live so I can stay up half the night and read it! I was THAT EXCITED! And let me tell you all- it did not disappoint. The best book in the trilogy by far! <br/><br/>Before I get into my review, let me introduce you to my <b>favorite crazy man</b> JESSE WARD, and all his fabulous qualities that make me love him so! <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b6bef86c-1e01-41cc-909e-3e698fba7d73_zps3976d0ce.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790297.jpg' alt=' photo b6bef86c-1e01-41cc-909e-3e698fba7d73_zps3976d0ce.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>That about </span>
  <span id="freeText7989977693818195582" style="display:none"><b>5 Lord of the Manor Loving Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/7563fe7a-5665-4266-b8aa-7fcc7d40f0a1_zpsb654e5fb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790296.jpg" alt=" photo 7563fe7a-5665-4266-b8aa-7fcc7d40f0a1_zpsb654e5fb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So it’s Monday night at midnight... what am I doing? Thats right, I am awake clicking the refresh screen on amazon to see if ‘This Man Confessed’ is live so I can stay up half the night and read it! I was THAT EXCITED! And let me tell you all- it did not disappoint. The best book in the trilogy by far! <br><br>Before I get into my review, let me introduce you to my <b>favorite crazy man</b> JESSE WARD, and all his fabulous qualities that make me love him so! <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b6bef86c-1e01-41cc-909e-3e698fba7d73_zps3976d0ce.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790297.jpg" alt=" photo b6bef86c-1e01-41cc-909e-3e698fba7d73_zps3976d0ce.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That about covers it. Get ready to take a ride on the crazy train with Jesse and Ava! <br>This may not be a conventional review, but this isn’t an conventional book. I couldn’t possibly review it properly without spoiling the hell out of the story, so it will be a little un-proper. <br><br>At the end of ‘Beneath This Man’, Ava and Jesse decide to get married. That is right where ‘This Man Confessed’ starts off... If you think you know what is going to happen in this book, think again! There was so much drama, ups and downs, secrets, confessions, and one curveball after another. And I loved every single page! <br><br>Jesse Ward is not your average man. He is just AMAZING. All his little sayings that just make me squeal with delight! <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/79fff84a-a0aa-454f-b11d-229d6e68f8be_zpsb13b2611.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790298.jpg" alt=" photo 79fff84a-a0aa-454f-b11d-229d6e68f8be_zpsb13b2611.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Jesse is my favorite crazy mother fucker. I seriously love this man! He is perfection. I don’t care that he told Ava to watch her mouth over 25 times in this book- it’s endearing to me. I just can’t get enough of him! He was better in this book than ever. Jesse in the bedroom is like no other. He always has the power. Always. Anytime, anywhere. LOVE LOVE LOVE HIM!!! I really don’t see how people can say they don’t like Jesse... what is not to like??? <br><br>Now Ava on the other hand, Ava got under my skin in this book. There were times I wanted to throttle her. She really pissed me off. But she did redeem herself, so thats something. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/fcadc1c9-d6af-45ac-83f7-470be0fa8f14_zpsa74d23f9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790299.jpg" alt=" photo fcadc1c9-d6af-45ac-83f7-470be0fa8f14_zpsa74d23f9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ava and Jesse’s relationship has been tested more times than I care to count. They are strong together- if they can endure all they’ve been through, they can get through anything. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/713b570f-72e0-4bd7-82bc-51c33c91fc7b_zps64fcb2a3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790300.jpg" alt=" photo 713b570f-72e0-4bd7-82bc-51c33c91fc7b_zps64fcb2a3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I was finished with this book, I felt completely satisfied. I had no unanswered questions, the epilogue was perfection. I am a little sad that Jesse and Ava’s story is over, but I was so happy with how it ended. This is one of my favorite trilogies. It’s intense, beautiful, emotional and full of drama- Note to the author: I will read ANYTHING you write woman! ANYTHING! Such an amazing journey-<b> READ IT AND LOVE IT!!! END OF-</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6a1e3ffa-ca4f-476d-b75a-9ee3e04c13db_zps42de39fb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405572i/790301.jpg" alt=" photo 6a1e3ffa-ca4f-476d-b75a-9ee3e04c13db_zps42de39fb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>♥ ♥ ♥ A spectacular buddy read with Lisa Jayne and the Pink Ladies ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>‘Do you feel that?’ He flattens my palms on his chest and holds them there firmly. ‘It was made to love you, Ava. For too long it was useless, redundant, not required. Now it’s gone into overdrive. It swells with happiness when I look at you. It splinters with pain when we fight. And it beats wildly when I make love to you. Maybe I go overboard with my love, but that’s never going to change. I’ll love you this fiercely until the day I die, baby.’ </blockquote>
</i></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509586014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12842540101182969797"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasThisManConfessed3TitlebySueBee_zps58976f19.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405634i/790487.jpg' alt=' photo MalpasThisManConfessed3TitlebySueBee_zps58976f19.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/mcsteamy2bysb_zpsd9223db6.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386168910ra/7305979.gif' alt=' photo mcsteamy2bysb_zpsd9223db6.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! This Man Confessed, book 3 of 3. The conclusion of the in-control yet so out-of-control, Jesse Ward’s intense & imperious romance of Ava O’Shea. A whirlwind tale filled with secrets, lies, villains & suspense plus their captivating love!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Everything that happens between us is a result of the potent, sometimes poisonous, love we share. It pushes us to behave erratically and unreasonably— both of us.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>This Man Series is the intense, epic saga about Jesse Ward i</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12842540101182969797" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasThisManConfessed3TitlebySueBee_zps58976f19.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405634i/790487.jpg" alt=" photo MalpasThisManConfessed3TitlebySueBee_zps58976f19.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/mcsteamy2bysb_zpsd9223db6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386168910ra/7305979.gif" alt=" photo mcsteamy2bysb_zpsd9223db6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! This Man Confessed, book 3 of 3. The conclusion of the in-control yet so out-of-control, Jesse Ward’s intense &amp; imperious romance of Ava O’Shea. A whirlwind tale filled with secrets, lies, villains &amp; suspense plus their captivating love!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Everything that happens between us is a result of the potent, sometimes poisonous, love we share. It pushes us to behave erratically and unreasonably— both of us.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>This Man Series is the intense, epic saga about Jesse Ward in his relentless pursuit and seduction of interior designer, Ava O’Shea</b>. Their story is filled with covert pasts and hidden agendas! It’s truly a wild, bumpy and emotional ride loaded with intrigue and shockers, undiluted lust and mind-bending sex plus a compulsive and intense love. Be prepared to be swept away by their story!<br><br><u>Books in This Man series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484476053" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489155223" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Beneath This Man</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509586014" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man Confessed</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2137108028" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">With This Man</a></b><br><br>Jesse’s and Ava’s story started when a <b>laidback and reckless playboy Jesse Ward</b>, owner of the Manor, wealthy business man and sex god with debauchery as his middle name, met what he thought was his latest conquest, interior decorator, <b> Ava O’Shea</b>. Instead <b>he falls hard and fast and turns into a controlling, bossy, possessive, desperate and secretive alpha</b>. Book 1 and 2 follow them through the ups and downs of Jesse’s pursuit, in what can best be described as <b>Euphoric Angst</b>. <br><br>Jesse, though he demands full control and disclosure, has managed to keep many secret. Some which have been revealed throughout, but most have left us hanging. <b>This Man Confessed (book 3) will uncover them all!</b> Story picks up shortly after the ending of book 2, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489155223" rel="nofollow noopener">Beneath This Man</a>. <br><br>Follow Jesse and Ava as their relationship is tested time and time again. The suspense in this long-ish conclusion will keep you at the edge of you seat with much to be resolved; <b>New and old villains continue to stir havoc, lies are told and secrets revealed. There are intrigue, surprises, pain, angst, frustration and ultimately joy as their relationship develops and matures into sweet bliss, sprinkled with countless moments of everything that is sex with Jesse.</b> I will say no more. Their saga is best experienced.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasThisMan3HerobySueBee_zps98a67ca4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405634i/790488.jpg" alt=" photo MalpasThisMan3HerobySueBee_zps98a67ca4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Jesse Ward</b> is just what I needed. In fact he is everything that I needed! He has captivated and kept me on “Central Jesse Cloud Nine” throughout. He truly is all pure, sexy, unadulterated alpha! Six words to describe <b>Jesse: Intense, bossy, compulsive, enigmatic, possessive and elusive.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“The flawlessness of his beautiful face will amaze me until the day I die— his lightly tanned skin, his almost girly long lashes, the faint crease across his brow. It would take me a lifetime to run through all his stunning features. My devastating man, in all of his challenging ways.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasThisMan3HeroinebySueBee_zpsbe9d1793.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405634i/790489.jpg" alt=" photo MalpasThisMan3HeroinebySueBee_zpsbe9d1793.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Ava O’Shea</b> is everything that Jesse needed and everything we needed to keep the story going. She stood up to him, she succumbed to him, she riled him, she created more drama and she kept the mystery and story going by NOT demanding answers. Six words to describe <b>Ava; Talented, strong, focused, ambitious, stubborn and meek.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“My beautiful girl. My defiant temptress. My lady. My angel. My Ava.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>This Man Series has introduced us to all that is sex with Jesse (or fucks depending on the mood):<br><b>
  <i>Reminder fucks, Sleepy sex, Make friends sex, Shower fucks, Hangover sex, Catching up sex, Sense fucks, Seeing stars fucks, Apology fucks, Possessive fucks, Retribution fucks, Sleepy celebration sex, Alfresco fucks, Proposal fucks and Truth fucks. <br>And in this story we are introduced to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Compromise fucks, Quiet fucks and Sleepy twilight sex. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>Euphoric Angst! Intense! Suspenseful! Captivating! Memorable! Epic! What a way to end a series! Thanks for the extensive-ish epilogue from Jesse’s POV! Job well done Ms. Malpas!</b>
  <br>
  <br>
  <a>
    <blockquote>
      <i>
        <b>“You keep my heart beating, baby. And it will only ever beat for you.”</b>
      </i>
    </blockquote>
  </a>
</b><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+ stars <br>Heroine rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 5 stars<br>*********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes!<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20hands/tumblr_mr0gt8E0d81qg9t8yo1_500_zpsa962714e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386129091ra/7297229.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mr0gt8E0d81qg9t8yo1_500_zpsa962714e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13840783978852100235">"This Man Confessed" deserves 5++++++++++++ STARS!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps5ec6f2f6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405588i/790357._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps5ec6f2f6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Wow!!! Ms Malpas you are a GENIUS!!<br/>I truly loved the entire series!<br/>Jesse Ward will always be in my top five book boyfriend list.<br/>This last installment was sheer perfection.<br/>We get all of our questions answered in this book and the love shared between Jesse and Ava has evolved so much, it IS UNBREAKABLE!! :)<br/><br/>Jesse's over protectiveness with regards to the babies makes for a lot of the humor in this book and also just made him even more lovable.</span>
  <span id="freeText13840783978852100235" style="display:none">"This Man Confessed" deserves 5++++++++++++ STARS!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps5ec6f2f6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405588i/790357._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps5ec6f2f6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Wow!!! Ms Malpas you are a GENIUS!!<br>I truly loved the entire series!<br>Jesse Ward will always be in my top five book boyfriend list.<br>This last installment was sheer perfection.<br>We get all of our questions answered in this book and the love shared between Jesse and Ava has evolved so much, it IS UNBREAKABLE!! :)<br><br>Jesse's over protectiveness with regards to the babies makes for a lot of the humor in this book and also just made him even more lovable.<br>His need and total devotion for Ava is captivating.<br><br>"You've taken me completely,baby. You've swallowed me up and drowned me in your beauty and spirit. You know I can't function without you. You've made my life as beautiful as you are. You've made me want to live a worthy existence - a life with you. All I need is you - to look at you; to listen to you; to feel you. To love you."<br>"I need you to let me do all of those things, Ava. I need you to let me look after you forever."<br><br>"Let me see those eyes." I show him what he wants to see. " Why do you always demand to see them?" I ask.<br>He only smiles mildly, but his greens twinkle madly. "Because when I look into them, I know for sure that you're real."<br><br>These two complete each other. They can't exist without one another.<br><br>"Today I met you.<br>This day was the beginning of the rest of my life.<br>From this day I was your Ava, x."<br> <br>OMG I just loved that mural!!!! So,so, so romantic!!!!!<br><br>It is not only Jesse who is the obsessed one but also Ava. I loved that they knew each other so well.<br>I loved that Jesse knew what Ava was insecure about. Would he still love and desire her once she got bigger from the pregnancy? Would she still have his utter adoration once the baby was born?? You'd expect Jesse to have that worry, not Ava. It just made me love her more.<br><br>Finally the two completely understand each other and there is nothing the two can't overcome together.<br><br>Loved the Epilogue!!!! Perfect ending to a fantastic story.<br>I will hold Jesse and Ava in my heart forever!!! :)</span>

<div id="review_510449028" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510449028" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510449028?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone who loves alpha males!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510449028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12953513896108966802"><b>Fan-fucking-tastic, absolutely perfection!</b><br/><br/>**fans self** <br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_mammx7TQF21rsw1yf_zpsd5d1f806.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405765ra/790950.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mammx7TQF21rsw1yf_zpsd5d1f806.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Maybe I should let myself cool off a tad before writing this review.. Nah, I'll dive in while it's HOT. Yes, this book is HOT. If you loved Jesse Ward in This Man or Beneath This Man, I will be astounded if you don't fall fan-crazy in love with him more in This Man Confessed. He's still got his uber controlling (even more-so in ways) attitude and his "Ava, watch your fucking mouth" hang up but in this book, he's absolutely swoonworthy. </span>
  <span id="freeText12953513896108966802" style="display:none"><b>Fan-fucking-tastic, absolutely perfection!</b><br><br>**fans self** <br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_mammx7TQF21rsw1yf_zpsd5d1f806.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405765ra/790950.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mammx7TQF21rsw1yf_zpsd5d1f806.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maybe I should let myself cool off a tad before writing this review.. Nah, I'll dive in while it's HOT. Yes, this book is HOT. If you loved Jesse Ward in This Man or Beneath This Man, I will be astounded if you don't fall fan-crazy in love with him more in This Man Confessed. He's still got his uber controlling (even more-so in ways) attitude and his "Ava, watch your fucking mouth" hang up but in this book, he's absolutely swoonworthy. He's done a lot of growing up and he knows what he wants....a life with Ava and he will do anything to protect what's his.<br><br>So, when I started reading this little gem I was a tad.....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_mb8ysrouUI1r0dta6_zpsf6ffd421.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/651859.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mb8ysrouUI1r0dta6_zpsf6ffd421.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But it took absolutely zero time being a tad (or a LOT)....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_lyf989IhPX1qd2o39_zpsfa0da07d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405765ra/790951.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lyf989IhPX1qd2o39_zpsfa0da07d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But, being a totally SPOILER FREE REVIEW.... I must say there was a lot of....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_m6tpthzr5d1r5grla_zps5e408c8f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405765ra/790952.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6tpthzr5d1r5grla_zps5e408c8f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Hold onto your hats ladies, this book delivers a shit-ton of new information. All the Jesse secrets come out and new conflicts arise in their relationship. Rest assured, you will have a VERY difficult time putting this book down. It's rather long (yeah) and I ate up every word. When I was feeling all sweet and mushy from all of their romantic fluff- BAM, a new twist arises, knocking everything off its axis....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=incomingshitstorm_zps3a12a772.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405765i/790953.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book is a serious rollercoaster ride of emotions and you will love every minute of it!<br><br>In case you've forgotten the whole reason for swooning....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/c7f18a37acdbc4c5e3105278c90117e1_zps206d1e97.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405765i/790954._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo c7f18a37acdbc4c5e3105278c90117e1_zps206d1e97.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This books picks up sort of where Beneath This Man leaves off....Don't read spoiler if you didn't read the first two books, otherwise, you're safe reading. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they're getting MARRIED. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>It captures you from the get-go their love for each other. Jesse's need for Ava is borderline unhealthy. We all remember those missing pills..... no spoilers here.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/579004360c4c0e13d3a8116ca0dbcba4_zps901e9297.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405765i/790955._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 579004360c4c0e13d3a8116ca0dbcba4_zps901e9297.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I almost wish I had done a re-read of the first two books prior to diving into this. The main reason is there isn't a huge recap of previous events so I found myself thinking "Who was Matt...or Dan...What was Ruth Quinn's deal? What was up with Mikhail?" So if you don't remember those characters, do a re-read as they're back in full force!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/30b52fd80abf8880e4964ed66560493d_zps270dd443.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405765i/790956._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 30b52fd80abf8880e4964ed66560493d_zps270dd443.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For the size of the book, the pacing was awesome. It definitely wasn't like you were sitting back bored waiting for the next shoe to drop. It had a fair mixture of heat (more than fair share), suspense, OMFG moments, but in the end, it all ties together and you're left thinking "Why didn't I figure all this out before?" It's a full circle love story with all kinds of twists and turns. It's very hard to review this book as so much happens, I'm not leaking any spoilers. It needs to be experienced and I would refrain from reading a lot of reviews for that fear of those surprises ruining all the fun of it.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/918a25ec4e311fadced262280da9ba90_zpsa67db8bb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405765i/790957._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 918a25ec4e311fadced262280da9ba90_zpsa67db8bb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The ending is awesome. In fact, the epilogue is in Jesse's POV. Getting in his head was spectacular. Watching their story go full circle was one hell of a ride. This series will rank up there as one of my favorites for sure. <br><br> Did Ava make me uber upset at one point in this book? Hell yes, and you will know what I'm referring to when you get there in this book. But even she has grown up tenfolds over time and her unfailing dedication to their functionally dysfunctional relationship is commendable. As hot as Jesse is, his uber controlling borderline arsehole (shout out to Britishisms) nature would send most women for the hills.<br><br>So, go forth and enjoy this one. You won't soon forget it.....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/e12743208ff89f3c732ae7e8e1da9ea4_zps1d92c571.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405765i/790958._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo e12743208ff89f3c732ae7e8e1da9ea4_zps1d92c571.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_625597481" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=july-reads">july-reads</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=march-2018">march-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=series-book">series-book</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer625597481" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18065224459442473738">Reread on March 23- March 25/18<br/><br/>I’m so glad I reread this series in preparation for the new book that is now out! I can’t wait to see what Jesse and Ava have been up to in the last 16 years!!!<br/><br/>I was surprised at how many details I forgot since I’ve read this four years ago! One thing I do remember is the devotion that Jesse and Ava have for each other! Ava finally gets to prove her love several times in this instalment, and I am glad! It always seemed like Jesse cared more and Ava would run away a</span>
  <span id="freeText18065224459442473738" style="display:none">Reread on March 23- March 25/18<br /><br />I’m so glad I reread this series in preparation for the new book that is now out! I can’t wait to see what Jesse and Ava have been up to in the last 16 years!!!<br /><br />I was surprised at how many details I forgot since I’ve read this four years ago! One thing I do remember is the devotion that Jesse and Ava have for each other! Ava finally gets to prove her love several times in this instalment, and I am glad! It always seemed like Jesse cared more and Ava would run away at the sign of trouble. That wasn’t the case in book three!<br /><br />I could talk all day about this unique couple; but I’m so eager to get to the next book FINALLY!!!!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />We're not conventional baby.<br /><br /> But we're special. What we have is<br /> really special. You belong to me,and I<br /> belong to you. It just is. It's not natural<br /> for us to be apart, Ava."<br /><br />I loved being back in the crazy world of Jesse and Ava. Once again Jodi Ellen Malpas does not disappoint in creating a masterpiece full of hot sex, lots of drama, and a love that is loyal and true. The relationship of Jesse and Ava may not be normal to our eyes; but it is "their normal." I adore how they came to that conclusion, that they will never be like everyone else, and that is ok because they created their own bliss. The love and need that they have for one another was heart warming in my eyes, especially because I have watched them grow from the beginning of this often times; chaotic journey. The intensity that Jesse and Ave share is off the charts, and holy cow; the sex scenes in this book melt the words right off the pages!!!LOL! This couple darn well know how to make love and f**k on a whole new level then most. They indulge in all sorts of different types of sex again, but my favorite hands down was the new: "sleepy twilight sex."<br /><br />I was impressed that even though this was the last book, there was still a lot of loose ends that were tied up beautifully and reveals that were brought up right up until the very end. Some of those reveals were jaw dropping to say the least! There is never a dull moment in the world of Jesse and Ava. I will say that there was a point where I wanted to commit a murder with the way Ava was behaving. It was touch and go for awile there, and I swear I became so absorbed in the story and Ava's behaviour that if I could have bodily harmed her; I would have!! I am pleased to say that it took her awhile, but eventually she did smarten up! Thank Goodness for that, as I was about to have a heart attack! LOL <br /><br />There are only a few books where I become so absorbed in the story that I become so involved my emotions run away on me. This is one of them. I have to say that this was a bittersweet book for me, because I enjoyed it thoroughly-especially getting answers and even closure on a lot of situations. I am truly sad though to have to say goodbye to this unique couple. I will miss Jesse and his controlling,possessive ways. He is a character that I am sure will be very hard to beat.<br />I loved the epilogue that was done in his POV, and it was five years down the road. It was a pleasant surprise to get a glimpse of their life in the future. <br />Now with great sadness, I say goodbye to Jessa and Ava; and I wish them nothing but happiness, lots of sleepy sex, good times...and let us not forget...many jars of peanut butter!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18065224459442473738" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Keep your damn legs closed..too!!!...lol(you shouldn't want to think that in a "love" story) &amp; I think she might Be an alcoholic too!!...lol all her glasses of wine!!..she might as well set up a damn I.V. with it!!...lol but then again...if I had Jesse chasing after me...it would drive me to drink too!!!...lol &amp; when she finds out she's preggers... She gets all freaked out...ok... What did she think would happened when you don't take your pill &amp; have lots of Unprotected sex... How can you be so shocked! <br />what's even more disgusting is how she gets wasted!! Knowing she is pregnant!!( just to show him...cause she's upset about being pregnant!!)<br />She really doesn't put up a fight when Sarah comes back in the picture..hello!!! you walked in on her Whipping your man!!! But she forgave him &amp; blamed herself!!!lol<br />Ava is truly a walking door mat!!..<br />I mean...its like Jesse can do no wrong!...she can walk in on him Banging some chick on the kitchen table...&amp; she would forgive him &amp; blame herself for it...lol...ughhh<br />&amp; To further prove my point that Ava is a door mat... she doesn't even care that Jesse was married before &amp; had a kid!!!!... He lied to her!!<br /><br /> I mean this is not even a love story!!! At all!!<br /><br />&amp; Ava...how can she treat her brother like that!!! <br />Her brother has to ask permission to hug his own sister...(cause I'm sure her brother is just dying to get his hands all over his sister!! Oh please...) <br />Ava pissed me off when she treated her brother like that! She should have just got up &amp; hugged him...Ava treated her family like shit in this book...I hated it!<br /><br />Her Supposedly best friend Kate... Got on my last nerves! She's no best friend!! She takes Jesse side on everything!!!...<br />"He's really tore up", "hear him out", " he's hurting too"...who the f*** cares!!! Your supposed to be AVA's friend... Not his!!<br />she lets Ava get shit faced....&amp; she lets her get man handled...not once does Kate have a talk with her about leaving him... Or asking her if she thinks her relationship is normal...or try to hide her ass when Ava leaves him!!! or at least try to talk to her about the drinking while pregnant...&amp; even when she knows her friend is having a hard time with Jesse &amp; left him... she still keeps that damn Van Jesse got for her!!!!<br />what kind of friend is that!!<br /><br />Jesse is Manipulative, Domineering, a cheater, a Liar &amp; an asshole!... Oh yeah ...&amp; he's a stalker too!!! I just have 3 words for you...THE AVA WALL!!...he must have camera's all over his place...ughh... How can she not get freaked out about that!!<br /> I don't know how anybody could find him sexy...or say to them selfs... Oh yeah...now that's what I want in a guy!!!! He cheats on Ava for 4 days!!... Gets whipped by his psycho employee... Which he Lets go then hires back!!!..Drinks vodka until he blacks out!(blames her because its her fault that he drinks!!) mean while ..she can't even take a shit in peace... Lol....Because she's needs to ask permission!!..lol(I'm over exaggerating... But you get what I'm saying)...she can't do shit!!!!<br /> He's a poster child for abusive relationships!!!! Not sexy at all!!! He never wined and dined Ava...to me anyways...throwing her on the floor of a Restaurant &amp; telling her to tell him "I Love You" and mean it... Screams wining and dining...I mean who doesn't want to be laid out on a dirty floor with a bunch of people around... That's so romantic!!!<br />I can't even describe how much these books affected me...&amp; not in a good way either! <br />Seriously.....I do not even know how people can rate these book 5 stars!!! Truly unbelievable!!!<br />Ava has no say... For anything!!!.. She can't pick her food, She can't pick what she wears, She can't do her job, She can't drink(she has to do it behind his back), She can't go to the bathroom.... She can't ask questions, She can't talk, shit!!!.. She can't even take her birth control pills!!!!<br />How did she ever live her life before him!!!..lol<br /><br />Oh god... The wedding!!!<br />They get married at the Manor!! She hates that place... But that's where they say their "I do's"...how romantic of Jesse....To think of Ava on her very special day(yeah right)... He slaps some handcuffs on her... In front of her family... And throughout the whole wedding reception wont let her go!!!! Totally disrespects Ava's parents!!!... He just doesn't give a shit!!! I mean who wouldn't want a wedding like that!!!!...he didn't even want to take pictures!!..<br /><br />These books were truly disgusting!!! <br />I seriously don't know how people find these books appealing...<br />I really don't know what the Author was thinking when she was Writing these books...I mean... Does she really think that all the shit Jesse does is sexy??!! <br />The whole...<br />"fuck some sense into her".<br />"Who has the power"<br />"Ava, watch your f****ing Mouth"<br />-He looks a little surprised at my lack of disobedience. "Good girl"<br />-He smiles down at me."yes. Do you see how happy you make me when you do what you're told?"<br />(Cause every girl loves to hear that!..lol)<br />-"Ava, I'm not sure how I feel about our babies taking to your breast."<br />(OMFG...give me a break!!!)<br />-Ava calling Jesse her GOD &amp; her lord... (Which probably wouldn't bug me...if he wasn't such a douche &amp; If she wasn't such a stupid idiot)<br />-Towards the end of the book...I truly feel she just gives up... Fighting... Because she knows she can't get anywhere...she just agree. &amp; their son sounds just like his dad!!! Great... Just what we need on the world... Another guy verbally abusing a woman!!<br /><br />Oh god... <br />It's like the author picked up a book about Verbal and physical abuse &amp; tried to write a love story!!!...lol<br /><br />I like to read books that I can imagine myself in or wish that I can be in their situation...<br />Pshhh...not in these books!!!<br />I would be running for a restraining order &amp; see if I can be put in the witness protection program to get away from Jesse!!!....lol<br />These 3 books were a train wreck!!!<br />I'm pissed off &amp; disgusted!<br />I know my review is all over the place... But I just had to get it all out!!...lol<br />Over all...I just wish I can get my $$ back &amp; my time that I invested in reading these books!!!! I wasted a weekend!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12075090192590775625"> <b>5 “What A Crazy and Awesomely Sexy Ride” Stars</b>	<br/><br/>Let me just deep breathe for some seconds. <br/><br/> <i>*inhale*, *exhale*</i><br/><br/>God, this was a hell of a ride.<br/>If you thought they couldn’t be worse than in the previous books, well, you are thoroughly mistaken. <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386111108ra/7293820.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book starts two weeks after the end of Beneath This Man, so if you've read the series you know what’s happening. And yes, it is a pretty beautiful part of this book.<br/>Unfortunately, it lasts very little time and soon the psychoses of both characters retu</span>
  <span id="freeText12075090192590775625" style="display:none"> <b>5 “What A Crazy and Awesomely Sexy Ride” Stars</b>	<br><br>Let me just deep breathe for some seconds. <br><br> <i>*inhale*, *exhale*</i><br><br>God, this was a hell of a ride.<br>If you thought they couldn’t be worse than in the previous books, well, you are thoroughly mistaken. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386111108ra/7293820.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book starts two weeks after the end of Beneath This Man, so if you've read the series you know what’s happening. And yes, it is a pretty beautiful part of this book.<br>Unfortunately, it lasts very little time and soon the psychoses of both characters return: and in full force. <br>Jesse’s possessiveness and controlling issues are annoying Ava more than ever and Ava… well, she just have the gift of driving Jesse crazy. Not always in a good way.<br>In this final book of their story, we have new “things” happening that will change completely the course of their lives and we start to unravel the mystery of Jesse’s past. <br>And if a lot of things will change, there’s one that always remain the same: their feelings for each other and their physical connection.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398365ra/769799.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I could never fall for a guy like Jesse in real life. I mean, I would want to kill him in the first five minutes, and then would run away and never look back. But as a book character he is a great alpha male. Not to mention sexy as sin. <br>Ava is pretty good too although SO frustrating. Not that I can blame her, they both are. <br>In overall, considering the story line, the character development and just how the book made me feel in general (crazy, but SO ADDICTIVE!) this is definitely a series worth reading.<br>I can’t believe I waited for so long to read it. <br><br>Now, I have to take a break or something and go read some Sesame Street books, because this left emotionally tired and drained. <br>And I think I’ve caught some of their craziness. This is more or less how I’m feeling in this moment;<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386111108ra/7293821.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Goodbye. <br>For now. (Obviously!)</span>
