<span id="freeTextContainer101159056995835658">Holy freaking cow!! What an amazing ending to a fan-freaking-tastic series!!! I don't think I can be in love with Jesse any more than I am right now!!! AH-mazing!! I just finished and I'm already having withdrawals. I love Jesse and Ava and am so sad the trilogy is over.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405661i/790567._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The third, and sadly last book in this series picks up right after Beneath This Man ends. Ava has agreed to marry her Lord, and Jesse being his neurotic self he needs this to happen sooner rather than later. So everything is put</span>
  <span id="freeText101159056995835658" style="display:none">Holy freaking cow!! What an amazing ending to a fan-freaking-tastic series!!! I don't think I can be in love with Jesse any more than I am right now!!! AH-mazing!! I just finished and I'm already having withdrawals. I love Jesse and Ava and am so sad the trilogy is over.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405661i/790567._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The third, and sadly last book in this series picks up right after Beneath This Man ends. Ava has agreed to marry her Lord, and Jesse being his neurotic self he needs this to happen sooner rather than later. So everything is put together quick and a beautiful ceremony takes place at, you guessed it, The Manor.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405661i/790568._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You've taken me completely, baby. you've swallowed me up and drowned me in you beauty and spirit. You know I can't function without you. You've made my life as beautiful as you are. You've made me want to live a worthy existence-a life with you. All I need is you-to look at you; listen to you; to feel you. To love you. I need you to let me do all of these things, Ava. I need you to let me look after you forever."</i>
</b><br><br>I can't say the whole day goes without a hitch, but that's about all the spoiler I'll give away for the day except, Jesse does a little jig on the dance floor. Admit it, every time Jesse dances some JT you totally get this in your head right?!?! :) <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405661ra/790569.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405661ra/790570.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As you gathered over the last two books, Ava keeps "losing" her birth control pills. I hope I'm not spoiling anything here, but it was sorta obvious that wasn't the case. This just ends up being obstacle one for Ava and Jesse. It was so hard for me to read parts of this, but I did understand the confusing situation. I almost feel like if I tell much more of this I could be spoiling so I think I will opt out, haha.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405661ra/790571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I'll just give you a hint of all of the excitement...car chases, scorned lovers, crazy deliveries from unknown people, of course, Jesse and Ava seem to get in their own way, break ins, admirers that go too far, meddling families, and so many confessions it will make your head spin but at the same time will make everything come together and explain Jesse so much better. And even one episode of Jesse running out of peanut butter, GASP, lol!! Don't kid, this is a serious thing for Jesse. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405661i/790572._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Do you feel that? It was made to love you, Ava. For too long it was useless, redundant, not required. Now it's gone into overdrive. It swells with happiness when I look at you. It splinters with pain when we fight. And it beats wildly when I make love to you. maybe I go overboard with my love, but that's never to to change. I'll love you this fiercely until the day I die, baby. ~~I'll never stop loving you hard. It'll only get harder because every day that passes we create more memories. My mind is being filled with beautiful images of us, and they are replacing a history that lingers. They're chasing away my past, Ava.</i>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405661ra/790573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Like I keep raving about, this series was amazing!! I see an opportunity for maybe a spin off with Dan?? Maybe Sam and Kate?? Or even Drew?? I honestly think Dan is the best bet out of these though.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405661i/790574.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Jesse and Ava still had scorching chemistry. Jesse and his sexy mouth can be just plain swoon worthy. The one thing I found hilarious was how he didn't want Ava swearing but he would turn right back around and swear right back at her while getting on to her. I love how Ava tried to keep her independence from him, but at the same time some of it was just childish on both ends, lol. I guess that's just them being crazy in love, they actually drove each other crazy, lol!!<br> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405661ra/790575.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Obviously don't read this book if you haven't read the other two first, but if you love over the top crazy possessive alpha men with dark pasts who fall in love with a woman who tries them at every turn even though she's madly in love with him and fight multiple obstacles together, this is totally the series for you. There was drama at every turn, either from Jesse's past or from Jesse and Ava themselves. It takes some time, but eventually they figure everything out and are determined that as long as they are together they can conquer anything/everything. Even if Jesse has to pay someone off, beat someone down, or come up with some kind of F@ck to make it right, he'll trample anyone who tries to come between them and will do it wherever, whenever and to whoever he feels it necessary and I love him all the more for it!! <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405661i/790576.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I want everything in the world with you, baby, and I want it all yesterday."</i>
</b><br><br><br>From before it was released, lol....<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405661ra/790577.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> I NEED THIS BOOK NOW, YESTERDAY EVEN, Why oh Why must I wait for this. I suppose I'll take a chill pill and hang her in the swings with this coo dude until then....<br><br><br><br></b></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/514037107?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer729961197164513350">**Excited**<br/><br/><blockquote>

  <b>Five 'Everything happens for a reason....' Stars</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>I'm struggling to find the words, my brain feels like it's had a work out and my Heart is fit to burst.....I cried and sobbed......just WOW.....this series has given me one of the best reading experiences <i>EVER.</i></b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Let me give you a flavour.....and share the love. ♥ ♥ ♥</i>

He's dominant, controlling, stro</span>
  <span id="freeText729961197164513350" style="display:none">**Excited**<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794880i/598043.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><i>
  <b>Five 'Everything happens for a reason....' Stars</b>
</i><br><br><b>I'm struggling to find the words, my brain feels like it's had a work out and my Heart is fit to burst.....I cried and sobbed......just WOW.....this series has given me one of the best reading experiences <i>EVER.</i></b><br><br><b>
  <i>Let me give you a flavour.....and share the love. ♥ ♥ ♥</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406303i/792537._SX540_.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Miss Malpas has given us a gift, the gift of <i>Jessie Ward</i></b> He was <u>everything</u> we have come to know and LOVE and so, so much MORE!!!!! He's dominant, controlling, strong, protective, loving, caring, gentle, warm, vulnerable, playful, fun, witty, he made me laugh out loud many times with his antics and dialogue, just marvellous....ABSOLUTELY MARVELLOUS!!!!!!<br><br>And just for the record, so we're all clear....he's <b>♥MINE♥</b><br><br><i>
  <b>'My challenging man'</b>
</i><br><br>So, as the title suggests there are confessions to be had, many more <b>
  <i>CONFESSIONS,</i>
</b> more than I expected? Some things can be guessed (well I guessed one thing only) but others......<b>
  <i>WOW</i>
</b> is all I'm saying.<br><br>The revelations explain so much about our beloved Jessie. His extreme reactions and behaviour, the lengths he goes to in all areas of his life. <br><br>Jessie and Ava share a love and passion for each other that is physically and emotionally so powerful, it makes it truly beautiful to read and glimpse into their world.<br><br>Our intense <b>LOVE</b> story develops at the perfect pace, creating suspense and intrigue, lust and passion, and of course some <b>
  <i>HOT SIZZLING OFF THE SCALE SEXY TIMES.</i>
</b> Miss Malpas can certainly write about sex, all kinds of, <i>'flavoured'</i> sex!! **wink wink** <br><br><i>
  <b>'I've never tasted anything so good.'</b>
</i> **knickers on fire**<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>'My beautiful girl. <br>My defiant temptress. <br><a title="By Lies Thru a Lens  (Gemma Uploaded by tm) [CC-BY-2.0 (http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0)], via Wikimedia Commons" href="http://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/File%3AGemma_(8350620946).jpg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="128" alt="Gemma (8350620946)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380573931i/3115983.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>My lady. My Angel. My Ava.'<br> <b>♥All Mine ♥</b></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><i>
  <b>'You've made my life as beautiful as you are.'</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380573931i/3115984.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At times Ava was a little lost which made her frustrating, but I loved her anyway, she has charm and class and Britishness. And this book just oozes Britishness to perfection with the knickers and the bl**dy and so much more. <br><br>Of course we still had all the other characters we have come to love in this story, Kate, Sam, John and Drew, Sarah (not so much love for her) to name a few, new characters emerge and all of them are linked and weaved into the story so fabulously...it's truly magical. <br><br><br>And Jessie <i>isms,</i> there are many but my favourite.......<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380573931ra/3115985.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It was said as often as you would expect. And it made me smile. ♥<br><br><br>Miss Malpas gives us a real treat at the end of this book and it's the Epilogue, delicious and sweet and beautiful......Simply Stunning. And that is the best way to sum up this book and, in fact, the whole series and most importantly <i>
  <b>Jessie Ward.......<br><br><blockquote> Simply Stunning........End of. ♥ ♥ ♥</blockquote></b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380573931i/3115986.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>'Now I live. And it's only for you.'</b>
</i> ~ Jessie<br><br>********<br><br>♥ BR with the fabulously gorgeous Pink bestie Ladies, Barb &amp; Deanna....Lisa Jayne...Christy....Farah....Mammamia....<br>♥ We're sharing the love ♥<br><br><br>Ava picture attribution - By Lies Thru a Lens  (Gemma Uploaded by tm) [<a href="http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0" rel="nofollow noopener">CC-BY-2.0</a>], <a href="http://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/File%3AGemma_(8350620946).jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">via Wikimedia Commons</a><br><br></span>

<div id="review_739633187" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/739633187" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/739633187?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer739633187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10098020991583069121"><b>♦ Reread September 2014 ♦ </b><br/><br/><br/><b>3, 2, 1, Zero....End of!</b> <br/><br/>This is it...the end of the series and Wow...what a ride! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381773348ra/5289302.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story starts off only two weeks after <i>Beneath This Man</i> and if you've read that, you know what is happening. It is wonderful and...sooo beautiful. And then we get some Jesse confessions but we all knew it was coming. Even though Ava had a good idea, she still comes unglued and rightfully so. <br/><br/>They separate ~again~ and that leads to more drama ~again~ but now we have someone who is after</span>
  <span id="freeText10098020991583069121" style="display:none"><b>♦ Reread September 2014 ♦ </b><br><br><br><b>3, 2, 1, Zero....End of!</b> <br><br>This is it...the end of the series and Wow...what a ride! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381773348ra/5289302.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story starts off only two weeks after <i>Beneath This Man</i> and if you've read that, you know what is happening. It is wonderful and...sooo beautiful. And then we get some Jesse confessions but we all knew it was coming. Even though Ava had a good idea, she still comes unglued and rightfully so. <br><br>They separate ~again~ and that leads to more drama ~again~ but now we have someone who is after Ava. Naturally, Jesse flips out and unbelievable things take an even worse turn. <i>*It's scenes like this that make me keep reading this series.*</i> Because just when things seem bleak, something wonderful comes out of it. <br><br>There's even more confessions and we finally get to know *supposedly* all of Jesse's secrets and boy, are there some doozies! I would love to spill them all but I won't do that to you. ;)<br><br>This series is not for everyone though. It <i>is</i> over the top and ridiculous and never in a million years would I ever stand for someone like Jesse in real life but it does make for an interesting story. <br><br>The crazy thing ~for me~ wasn't even the over the top stuff...it was all the secrets. Mainly from Jesse but Ava kept things from Jesse as well. It's funny because in the beginning, it seems as if she's the normal one but the more we find out, the more we realize how similar they are. And just when you think all the secrets are out...there's more! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/633301.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Of course, there is ton of hot sex...I mean, we are talking about Jesse and he is very creative. The good thing is that even though they still name their types of sex (Love Sleepy Twilight Sex), the desperation is gone and they are truly making love. Don't worry...there's still plenty of passion and some rough and hard stuff! <br><br>And we do get a lot of answers. We find out about Sarah and Coral and Ruth and if Kate stays with Sam or if she goes with Dan? And who is Sally dating and finally, what in the heck is going on with Mikael! <br><br>I was shocked at some of the answers and not surprised at others. I love what Jesse did with The Manor and The Ava Wall. But...my favorite, <i>favorite</i> thing was the epilogue...that was quite lovely and what a great way to end the series! <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623931.gif" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ "It was made to love you, Ava. For too long it was useless, redundant, not required. Now it’s gone into overdrive. It swells with happiness when I look at you. It splinters with pain when we fight. And it beats wildly when I make love to you. Maybe I go overboard with my love, but that’s never going to change. I’ll love you this fiercely until the day I die, baby."<br><br>♥ "Central Jesse Cloud Nine."<br><br>♥ "Constant contact. Wherever, whenever."<br><br>♥ "I love our normal."<br><br>♥ "I don’t demand to see her eyes anymore. I don’t need to check she’s real. As long as my heart keeps beating, I’ll know that she is."<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10098020991583069121" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer510131233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11507939173540980449"><b>4 ish Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”You keep my heart beating, baby, but you can also make it fucking stop.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>My rating for this book ranges from rating the story itself and a rating for the epilogue. <br/><br/><b>3 Stars for the story<br/><br/>5 Stars for the epilogue</b><br/><br/>The story starts with the couple’s wedding day and then drops you off the love roller coaster as soon as you board. For the first half of the story Ava drove me insane but Jesse Ward <b>FINALLY</b> won my affections in this final installment, he was adorable and sexy th</span>
  <span id="freeText11507939173540980449" style="display:none"><b>4 ish Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”You keep my heart beating, baby, but you can also make it fucking stop.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>My rating for this book ranges from rating the story itself and a rating for the epilogue. <br><br><b>3 Stars for the story<br><br>5 Stars for the epilogue</b><br><br>The story starts with the couple’s wedding day and then drops you off the love roller coaster as soon as you board. For the first half of the story Ava drove me insane but Jesse Ward <b>FINALLY</b> won my affections in this final installment, he was adorable and sexy the whole book! <br><br>Sadly, Ava is still in danger and we soon find out that that there are three, yes three psychotic ex woman of Jesse’s past/present wrecking havoc on the couple. Jesse and big tough John are completely stumped as to who is threatening Ava’s life. <b>COME ON THREE CRAZY EXES?</b> Oh and add one crazy ex-husband and Ava's ex Matt to the mix and the story enters ridiculous territory.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406302873ra/10532604.gif" width="390" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”This Man has thrown everything at me, and I still don’t plan on going anywhere. Unbreakable.”</i>
</b><br><br>Jesse’s past is completely revealed and things get crazy for the couple. Luckily, their love can withstand any storm.<br><br>As for that epilogue, it was truly superb!<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492359778ra/22509059.gif" width="390" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I don't demand to see her eyes anymore. I don't need to check she's real. As long as my heart keeps beating, I'll know that she is. End of."</i>
</b><br><br></span>

I stop laughing immediately when he reaches between his suits and produces a <i>Guide to Pregnancy</i> manual.<br>‘In here.’ He holds it up sheepishly. ‘You should also be taking folic acid.’<br>I gape at the book being dangled in front of me and watch with a mixture of astonishment and amusement as he starts flicking through the pages. There are pages folded over at the corners, and I think I even see a glimpse of a passage highlighted with a neon pen.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_612009009" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/612009009" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/612009009?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer612009009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17187568937915395082">Jointly reviewed for Totallybookedblog.com<br/><br/><b>Gitte:</b> What an absolutely bloody perfect end to the crazy, emotional and passionate ride that was the ‘This Man’ trilogy. We’ve had so many theories and questions, and finally we’re let into some pretty heart breaking and tragic secrets. Secrets that answer every single question, and leaves us with an aching heart and a complete understanding of The Lord, The God, The Sexy and Cocky Man that is Mr Jesse Ward.<br/><br/>No spoilers from us as per usual, but you will</span>
  <span id="freeText17187568937915395082" style="display:none">Jointly reviewed for Totallybookedblog.com<br /><br /><b>Gitte:</b> What an absolutely bloody perfect end to the crazy, emotional and passionate ride that was the ‘This Man’ trilogy. We’ve had so many theories and questions, and finally we’re let into some pretty heart breaking and tragic secrets. Secrets that answer every single question, and leaves us with an aching heart and a complete understanding of The Lord, The God, The Sexy and Cocky Man that is Mr Jesse Ward.<br /><br />No spoilers from us as per usual, but you will LOVE the conclusion. It will have you melting, swooning, laughing and crying. Oh, and there are plenty of ‘WHAT?!’ moments too, moments that will have your heart racing and feeling fearful, at the same time. Jodi hit a homerun with Confessed. Pure class! This series just got better and better with each instalment and is without doubt one of my all-time favourite trilogies….and don’t get me started on how much I love Jesse….sigh!!!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I want everything in the world with you, baby, and I want it all yesterday.” </i>
</b>- Jesse<br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> Couldn't agree more Gitte. What a brilliant end to a trilogy we have both completely devoured. And you're spot on, because this Trilogy had it all. Questions, intrigue, passion (oh dear god…the PASSION!) - I had so many conspiracy theories going into this installment, my head was spinning. And we were afforded all the answers we've been dying to get to the bottom of. Yep, EVERYTHING was answered and we were handed a whole heap more as well.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You keep my heart beating, baby. And it will only ever beat for you. Understand?"</i>
</b><br /><br />No spoilers at all! Everyone needs to experience This Man Confessed in the way the author intended it and I truly hope readers are afforded the opportunity to do just that because I can tell you there were a lot of surprises for me - I did a lot of OMFG's, cried, laughed and fanned myself. What a fantastic read this was. And yes, one of my favorite trilogies that's for sure!<br /><br />In This Man Confessed we have Mr Ward at his trampling best. Sweet baby Jesus….. that man! I'm devoid of enough words to describe him.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Oh yes, there he is, my husband, looking like he's just landed from planet fucking perfect."</i>
</b><br /><br />Indeed he did. And he took the express flight to planet perfect at that! Even though I wanted to throttle The Lord of The Manor at the start of This Man Confessed, this man made me laugh, cry and floored me with his tenderness and love. I can't say enough how much I love this man!<br /><br /><b>Gitte: </b>So, we start with a wedding, a wedding done Jesse style and we all know what that involves; trampling, controlling behaviour and bucket loads of passion and emotions.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“This man stops me breathing when he touches me and fucks me until I’m delirious. I can’t wait to marry him.”…”He used to cripple me with just his touch. Now he cripples me with his touch and his words. I’m destined for a life of crippling pleasure, melting tenderness and heart stopping emotion. He’s going to incapacitate me at every turn.” </i>
</b>– Ava<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Do you feel that?.....It was made to love you, Ava…It swells with happiness when I look at you. It splinters with pain when we fight. And it beats wildly when I make love to you. Maybe I go overboard with my love, but that’s never going to change. I’ll love you this fiercely until the day I die, baby.”</i>
</b> - Jesse<br /><br />So expect to be happily sitting back enjoying that ‘Mario’s Most Marvellous’, watching this happy event unfold whilst completely crushing and clenching. Then….bam the floodgates open and the reader gets swept away in crashing currents of intensity; a thrilling eye opening ride that has so many high’s and low’s by the end I was exhausted. The epilogue though…BEST EVER!! It was GENIUS which you’ll read for yourself! Jodi surpassed any expectations I had and she just nailed it. After three books of drama, obsession, tragedy and passion, I finished with THE biggest smile on my face and tears of laughter still rolling down my cheeks….Actually some of those may have been from the impending loss of leaving behind Ava &amp; Jesse too.<br /><br />Both Jesse and Ava do some real soul searching, and I suppose, come to realise their own faults and limitations. Ava comes into her element and her strength shines in Confessed. A true heroine. As for Jesse, he just astounds me.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“We’re not conventional baby. But we’re special. What we have is really special. You belong to me, and I belong to you. It just is. It’s not natural for us to be apart, Ava.” </i>
</b>- Jesse<br /><br />Aaaaah, Jesse, well we all know he’s challenging, controlling and obsessive. But I love him for it; Ava loves him for it. The two of them circle each other through the magnetic pull between them. Neither can leave the other alone, never mind over long periods of time. Despite Ava trying to assert herself, needing the distance to sort her head out. The pair of them piss the other off at no end. In reality though, they need each other to breathe, to survive and to live.<br /><br />In Confessed we see Jesse’s vulnerability, his intense need to protect what’s his because of his past. We see and feel his turmoil and understand his struggles. Some scenes had me in absolute tears as he exposes that vulnerability and uncertainty to Ava.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You keep my heart beating, baby, but you also make it fucking stop….You said you couldn’t live without me…Then stop trying to kill me off.”</i>
</b> – Jesse<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“This woman is my fucking life.”</i>
</b> - Jesse<br /><br />Jesse also made me laugh so much in this instalment. I highlighted like crazy but for fear of spoiling the final visit with them, I can’t stick the highlights in here. Just know that this man is on bloody fire with his banter, his thoughts and his wise cracks. That, added to his passionate, arrogant and controlling alpha maleness…well…how on earth can you resist him?!<br /><br />We find out just why Jesse is the way he is. Not immediately though. We still go through him hiding his past which consequently leaves Ava hiding things from him too. It all comes to a head as people are revealed for who they are and a thrilling drama ensues along with some pretty devastating truths.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Why did you do it?”</i>
</b> – Ava<br /><br />Because I love you….Everything is because I love you.” - Jesse<br /><br />Both Ava and Jesse frustrated me at times, they both make mistakes and their decisions are clouded by intense emotions, guilt and regret but ultimately love. However, the pair of them reminded me so many times why I adore and love them as much as I truly do. They are unbreakable!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Tell me why the fucking hell you did this to me!” </i>
</b>- Ava<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Because I wanted to keep you forever.”</i>
</b> – Jesse<br /><br />There are just so many ‘melt your heart into a puddle’ moments in Confessed.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Today my heart started beating again. Today you became mine.”</i>
</b> – Jesse<br /><br />If you ever doubted the love Jesse and Ava have for each other, well doubt no more. These two will always have a special place in my heart as will Jodi for giving them their voices. Blindingly brilliant conclusion to a fantastic series…FAB-U-LUSH Author!!!<br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> I have to start by reiterating what you said about THAT EPILOGUE! Honestly, it was one of THE best epilogues I have read. It exceeded all expectations and I loved it so much I had to go back and read it again straight away. Perfection!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"There are a million things about this man that make me despair, but there are endless things that make me adore him. Some of those despairing things I even adore."</i>
</b><br /><br />Now Gitte, you and I always chat about books as we're reading them and again when we've finished and we have burned up the phone lines throughout this series and no more so than during and after reading This Man Confessed. We can tell you readers...you will NOT be disappointed in how this series wraps up. Jodi Ellen Malpas has done a stellar job in this Trilogy and talk about bringing it home in this one! Well done Ms Malpas! A true winner! We are still discussing elements of this book and laughing or crying as we do so. Just brilliant!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Knock yourself out, baby. But please, let's just make this one a verbal trample."</i>
</b><br /><br />We learn so much about the man himself. So much clicked into place in this installment. Some revelations astounded me, some shocked me, some crushed me. Some I saw coming, some completely blindsided me and I definitely ran the gamut of emotions throughout this whole book.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"…right now when he's pouring his love into me through our mouth contact, is his way of finding the strength. It's his way of ensuring that I'm real before he off loads a past of pain."</i>
</b><br /><br />The passion between Jesse and Ava is second to none. You feel every emotion, get hot and bothered over the physical exchanges because these two totally burn up the pages and have a front row seat through all their ups and downs. Ava and Jesse are learning about one another and naturally mistakes are made along the way.<br /><br />To see the growth of these characters throughout the series. To witness their struggles, their heated exchanges, their heartbreaking moments and to have it all culminate and conclude in this outstanding book....just wonderful!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I don't know how I ever survived without this. I existed, Ava. I didn't live."</i>
</b><br /><br />Jesse and Ava gave me their all. You feel with every breath you take that theirs is a love to withstand all. The heat, the passion, the intensity, the hilarious banter - these two had me in fits -and Jesse's humour was on fire! Their tender moments…sigh…talk about melting your heart.<br /><br />I'm still on Central Jesse Cloud Nine and I may never leave! Once again I have to agree with my blog buddy. This Man Confessed. Was. Brilliant. Just. Bloody. Brilliant. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"And no more confessions because I have nothing left to tell."</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>ARC supplied by author in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer12436125900622300145"><br/><br/>Let's begin...<br/><br/><b>ONE....<br/><br/><br/>TWO...<br/><br/><br/>THREE...</b><br/><br/>What a fantastic ending to the end of this wonderful series!!!!<br/>Ill be first to admit that this, Jesse and Eva frustrated me at times during this series but now knowing what I do... Everything makes perfect sense and all his actions were somewhat <b>Justified-<i>ish</i></b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>I wouldn't have my Lord, my Sex God, any other way!!!!!</u>

  <span id="freeText12436125900622300145" style="display:none"><br><br>Let's begin...<br><br><b>ONE....<br><br><br>TWO...<br><br><br>THREE...</b><br><br>What a fantastic ending to the end of this wonderful series!!!!<br>Ill be first to admit that this, Jesse and Eva frustrated me at times during this series but now knowing what I do... Everything makes perfect sense and all his actions were somewhat <b>Justified-<i>ish</i></b><br><br><b>
  <u>I wouldn't have my Lord, my Sex God, any other way!!!!!</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406824i/794135.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm just glad that I gave this series the time it deserved and Jodi Ellen Malpas did an excelled job in keeping every single one of us Intrigued, Aroused (a lot of the time), frustrated, confused and made us all feel a whole lot of love for This man...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406824i/794136._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Questions were answered and finally we understand This man and his over controlling ways..<br><br>This Man Confessed, WOW of WOW this book, words cannot describe the way I felt. I was sad, happy, totally in love, Totally turned on and left in a pool of Sappyness (is this even a word?)<br>This is what this Man does to me!<br><br><b>
  <i>"You’ve taken me completely, baby. You’ve swallowed me up and drowned me in your beauty and spirit. You know I can’t function without you. You’ve made my life as beautiful as you are. You’ve made me want to live a worthy existence—a life with you. All I need is you—to look at you; to listen to you; to feel you.’</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406824i/794137.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ava, the girl I screamed at a lot for her stupidity throughout this series, she completely amazed me with her strength and Love towards This man.<br><br>Ava finally understood the reasoning behind this controlling, crazy and arrogant ways but honestly I wouldn't have it any other way...<br><br>These two, no matter that they had to face are destined to be together, through the good, the bad and the ugly...<br>They are Soul Mates to the Core and its quite evident that they are the reason that each other lives, they keep each others hearts beating....<br><br><b>
  <i>"It was made to love you, Ava. For too long it was useless, redundant, not required. Now it’s gone into overdrive. It swells with happiness when I look at you. It splinters with pain when we fight. And it beats wildly when I make love to you. Maybe I go overboard with my love, but that’s never going to change. I’ll love you this fiercely until the day I die, baby."</i>
</b><br><br>Their Passion and potty mouths and ridiculous fights and every single crazy thing in between was soooo. Worth it!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406824ra/794138.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I didn’t tell you how beautiful you look.’ ‘I thought it, but my beautiful girl renders me stupid every time I lay my eyes on her. It’s like I’m looking at her for the first time all over again.’ 'You keep my heart beating, baby. And it will only ever beat for you...</i>
</b><br><br>I love Jesse Ward and all his kind of fucks that go with him and Challenging ways!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"You feel so fucking good. I don’t know how I ever survived without this. I existed, Ava. I didn’t live.’"<br>"Now I live. And it’s only for you.’</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406824ra/794139.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No way will I defy him. He can truly have me <b>
  <i>Wherever, Whenever....</i>
</b><br><br><br>That Epilogue!!!! Fcuking Hell!!!<br>Pure Perfection!!!!!<br>Fot sure this was one of Thee Best Epilogue's I've EVER READ!<br><br>I am in <b>Central Jesse Cloud Nine!</b><br><br>Nothing else so say except that Jesse Ward will never be forgotten...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406824i/794140._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I don’t demand to see her eyes anymore. I don’t need to check she’s real."<br><br>"As long as my heart keeps beating, I’ll know that she is."</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406824i/794141.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nothing less than 5 BRILLIANT STARS<br><b>End Of. </b></span>

It swells with happiness when I look at you. It splinters with pain when we fight. And it beats wildly when I make love to you. Maybe I go overboard with my love, but that’s never going to change. I’ll love you this fiercely until the day I die, baby.'</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Can you guys believe it? :O I LIKED AND VERY MUCH ENJOYED THIS BOOK. :P<br>So let me start of by saying, I enjoyed this book far more than I could have imagined. It was wayh better than the first two books!<br>I hated the first two books, because quite frankly it was shit. Totally draged out and giving out nothing kinda shit. But this book?<br><br>BEAUTIFUL!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/644380.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="smile" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But then again, most of the things did piss me off... a LOT.<br><br><b>
  <u>The annoying parts!!<u></u></u>

Get a grip you two looney bins.<br><br>They were like overgrown kids in a relationship. His controlling nature wasn't even normal! I MEAN FOR FUCKS SAKE WARD. <b>YOU KNOW A PERSON IS INSANE WHEN HE HANDCUFF'S HIS WIFE ON THE WEDDING DAY</b><br><br><i>Lets make friends</i> if anyone says that to me... ever, GOD HELP THEM.<br><br>THEY PULL EACH OTHER'S HAIR. I have never done that in my entire childhood, forget ever doing it later on.<br><br>The epilogue; No children talk that way. At least be realistic on that part author.<br>Read the whole book for the kids and then what do we get? JUST A FUCKING STUPIDLY ANNOYING EPILOGE.<br><br><br><b>
  <u>The good parts!!<u></u></u>
</b><br>I liked the story drama of this book. NOT the emotional drama.. because that was just over the top but the whole story drama of this book was pretty good! I enjoyed it<br><br>LOVED IT. We got sooooo many answers, all the answers to the questions which filled my head.<br>This book had crazy drama, and e amazing story *yes, I know.. was shocked myself!!* and a beautiful HEA~ :D<br><br>Jesse calmed the fuck down at last in this book, He was totally less insane compared to the first two books. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>‘And I have arms, and they were made to hold you.’</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't want to add more quotes or anything, because they will be major spoilers. Just trust me and read this book even if you didn't enjoy book 1 &amp; 2, you won't regret it! :D</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509200526" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1736607947999877424"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790308._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>*** 5 Central Jesse Cloud Nine Stars ***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790309._SY540_.jpg' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>Jesse-- "Tell me what you want, baby."<br/>Ava-- "Just you. However you come."<br/>Jesse-- "I come with uncontrollable love for you. Is that good enough?"<br/>Ava-- "It's good enough."<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Things seem to be going smoothly for Jesse and Ava. She knows she will never be able to completely tone down the control freak in him, but she knows he his trying to be better</span>
  <span id="freeText1736607947999877424" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790308._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>*** 5 Central Jesse Cloud Nine Stars ***</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790309._SY540_.jpg" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>Jesse-- "Tell me what you want, baby."<br>Ava-- "Just you. However you come."<br>Jesse-- "I come with uncontrollable love for you. Is that good enough?"<br>Ava-- "It's good enough."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Things seem to be going smoothly for Jesse and Ava. She knows she will never be able to completely tone down the control freak in him, but she knows he his trying to be better for her. Soon, Ava finds out more about Jesse involving his past. Can she accept Jesse and all of his secrets? Or will she walk away from the only happiness she has ever had?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh Jesse... just when I think I can't possibly love you more... <b>I FREAKING DO!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790310.jpg" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You've taken me completely, baby. You've swallowed me up and drowned me in your beauty and spirit. You know I can't function without you. You've made my life as beautiful as you are. You've made me want to live a worthy existence -- a life with you. All I need is you -- to look at you, to listen to you, to feel you. To love you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This man had me wanting all he was willing to give:<br>♥ Sleepy sex or sleepy twilight sex<br>♥ The countdown<br>♥ Sense fuck<br>♥ Retribution fuck<br>♥ Etc, etc.<br><b>I WANT IT ALL!!</b> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"If I want to fuck you hard and make you scream, then I will. If I want to make love to you, Ava, and make you purr, then I will.... You are mine, so I'll do what I like with you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He was so über sweet. I could not stop swooning. The things that this man would say! <b>*sigh*</b> But don't worry. He was still plenty demanding and oh so yummy. He was also a barrel of secrets that were finally revealed. We get to see <i>who</i> Jesse really is and <i>why</i> he is the way he is. Like I mentioned in my review of the previous book, I love it when Jesse opens up to Ava. I melted completely. He loves Ava so much that, <i>yeah</i>, it can be a bit too much at times but I absolutely adore him for being that way. I know alot of people think he is crazy <b>(and I admit, I thought he kinda was too)</b>, but now that I understand him, I think he is just plain wonderful! I <b>LOVE</b> him! <b>End of.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445451389ra/16652128.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jesse may not have seemed so freaking insane in this book, but the story made up for it by introducing some pretty cray cray characters. I couldn't believe the madness that was occuring. It was more entertaining than watching a soap opera. There were moments where I was literally shocked by what was happening. I was speechless. There were just so many things we had yet to learn about Jesse's past. As well as the twists that occured. <b>It was AWESOME!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790311._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"We're not conventional, baby. But we're special. What we have is really special. You belong to me, and I belong to you. It just is. It's not natural for ust to be apart, Ava.... This is where you're supposed to be."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Ava finally turned around a bit for me. Although, in the beginning of this book, I totally disliked her. She was so annoying and selfish. But once she saw the light, I actually started to like her. She stuck with Jesse through thick and thin. I greatly appreciated her doing that instead of running away. She even took care of him when he needed it. It was so lovely to see that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/532706.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I don't demand to see her eyes anymore. I don't need to check she's real. As long as my heart keeps beating, I'll know that she is. End of.<br><br>--Jesse<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The ending was <b>SO</b> friggin beautiful! I didn't want it to end. I will miss my crazy neurotic lovable Jesse. I just love him too much!! I was so happy with how everything concluded for them. I felt the series became better with each book. I swooned, I laughed, I teared up, I got angry, and I smiled so big. It was a fantastic read, and if you love Jesse as much as I do.... <b>YOU HAVE TO READ THIS BOOK!!</b> </span>

  <span id="freeText14438539827529496000" style="display:none">5 - <b>"We're not conventional, baby... But we're special."</b> Stars!<br><br><b>

  <u>Original review from 2013.</u>
</i><br>I am not going to write a great long essay about this book, not going to tag 100's of pictures to it, and dozens of JPegs, because quite frankly they get on my nerves when I read see them in other reviews so much I skip right by, and to be honest I have better things to do with my life. <br><br>This book blew me away, there were shocks, thrills and spills galore. I cried, laughed, sighed and shouted in equal measure. I keep my reviews spoiler free and as such will just say, if you enjoyed books 1 &amp; 2 you are going to be on Central Jesse Cloud Nine when you read this, Jodi has done our boy proud(sorry to steal him JEM). I can hands down say this is the best ending to a series of books I have read so far, there wasn't anything else I would have wanted to see, and the epilogue is panty-droppingly awesome!!! <br><br>I was around at the beginning of the This Man phenomenon, and I am so happy that Jodi Ellen Malpas has secured a publishing deal for this wonderful trilogy of books. I CANNOT wait to hold all three in hard-copy in my hands when they are released next year, and I look forward to seeing where Jodi's authourly talents take us all next.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457954696i/18425325._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11212959885151793331"><b>4 Stars<i> (Originally Read - 1/13/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b>3 Stars<i> (Re-Read - 1/23/2020)</i></b><br/><br/>I'm not going to do my full review format because I skimmed most of this and I don't want to give any incorrect information. I wanted to complete the trilogy but was convinced I wouldn't enjoy it (like I did years ago when I first read it) based on my experience re-reading the previous two. <br/><br/>I'm glad I at least skimmed it though. I feel as though much more happened in this one than in the 2nd book, and I enjoyed the epilogue. I rem</span>
  <span id="freeText11212959885151793331" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars<i> (Originally Read - 1/13/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b>3 Stars<i> (Re-Read - 1/23/2020)</i></b><br /><br />I'm not going to do my full review format because I skimmed most of this and I don't want to give any incorrect information. I wanted to complete the trilogy but was convinced I wouldn't enjoy it (like I did years ago when I first read it) based on my experience re-reading the previous two. <br /><br />I'm glad I at least skimmed it though. I feel as though much more happened in this one than in the 2nd book, and I enjoyed the epilogue. I remembered really liking it, and I'm glad I at least read that. It gave good closure and a sweet HEA. <br /><br />So! If you enjoyed the first two books, I'd recommend finishing them off with this one because I think it's probably the best out of the three.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11212959885151793331" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('c5m8chOJczI+JeRx0cPPjukaQ26IUAiIVBwCdQh7ae5Jv9WgqNe6WpkOUBAmNsVRP0Wkpkbdhu8PYkTExTibdA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Teq3dg7vnH8yruAGMD+g9bVLddUqBfuHJz14GgURMX93zN6ktbFVF5WFVGfHyqoqYxSSHeSIdeB8Qz6ryFLD5Q==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4377991684101640583">‘A lingering idea that I just couldn’t ignore.’ – Jodi Ellen Malpas<br/><br/>Jodi Ellen Malpas wrote her debut series, The This Man Trilogy, in secret, worried about what people might think if they knew what her imagination was capable of. She was shocked herself. But she finally found the courage to unleash her creative streak and self-published THIS MAN - the first book of the This Man Trilogy - in Octobe</span>
  <span id="freeText4377991684101640583" style="display:none">‘A lingering idea that I just couldn’t ignore.’ – Jodi Ellen Malpas<br /><br />Jodi Ellen Malpas wrote her debut series, The This Man Trilogy, in secret, worried about what people might think if they knew what her imagination was capable of. She was shocked herself. But she finally found the courage to unleash her creative streak and self-published THIS MAN - the first book of the This Man Trilogy - in October 2012. She took a chance on a story with a hero who soon became one of modern day fictions most prolific alpha male characters. <br /><br />Jesse Ward – also affectionately known as The Lord of The Manor, sparked incredible reactions from women across the globe and catapulted Jodi into the world of women’s fiction. With so much love and enthusiasm from her readers, and a thirst for more of her words, Jodi suddenly wasn't afraid of her imagination anymore. She went on to write The One Night Trilogy with the delectable and mysterious Miller Hart, and stole the hearts of her readers once again. She’s now a proud #1 New York Times bestselling author – all six of her published novels having hit the New York Times best sellers list – as well as a Sunday Times bestseller and international best seller. Her work is published in over 20 languages across the world. <br /><br />Jodi was born and raised in the Midlands town of Northampton, England, where she lives with her two boys and a beagle. She is a self-professed daydreamer, a Converse &amp; mojito addict, and has a terrible weak spot for Alpha Males.<br /><br />Writing powerful love stories and creating addictive characters has become her passion – a passion she now shares with her devoted readers<br /></span>
